< Name>
Jeffrey Hopkins (Jeffeo)<//Name>
<Date>1621430304186< /Date><Rate>1<//Rate><text>If you are thinking of buying this bike, read this entire review. There is no doubt in my mind you will feel my pain

The day it came, I put it together. It was a piece of cake! Adding the motor, the wheels, the oil, and the seat (everything else comes pre-assembled). It looked terrific when I finished. It started right up on the 3rd pull.

While getting going on my maiden voyage, I did not like the way the motor sounded. I was very clanky, and it sounded like something was grinding. Plus, I could run faster than it went. I shut it down right away. It turns out the motor was a dud.

The new engine came a couple of days later and it was great. It started right up and as soon as it was running; I knew it was going to be a good one. And I was right. I bypassed the governor to give me some better high-end speed. I did not drive it full throttle most of the time. I know that bypassing the governor can blow the engine if you abuse it too much.

After riding one day; I noticed 2 broken spokes on the rear wheel. I did not remember hitting any bumps that should have done that. I removed the spokes and called Gasbike to order new ones. Lorenzon told me they do not sell the spokes.

So now I'm riding with two missing spokes and hoping that only two missing would not be a problem. That night I rode up to 7/11 and as soon as I got there the rear wheel felt damaged. When I checked the wheel, there were now 8 more broken spokes! The bike was not ridable!
I had to order a new back wheel from Gasbike. It was a little more than $100.

All along, I am spending way too much time constantly adjusting the brakes. No matter what I do, I just can't get any consistency out of them.

About two months ago (I've had the bike for about 5 months) I go to start it up one day, and right after it starts, CLANK, BANG, BOING, the motor blows up. Kaput! It's a goner! I

Now, I have to pay $139 for a new engine. I spoke to Rosa about it and she said I need to speak to Lorenzo; he can work with me on the price. She says she will send him an email to call me right away. Two days later, no call yet. I already ordered the new motor and paid for it because I need the bike for work and had to get it back up and running ASAP.

I called Gasbike on the 3rd day and got Rosa again. She said she will tell him again to call me. No call. I call Gasbike again. Rosa will call him and have him call me right now! The call never came, and I gave up. I already installed the new motor and just dropped the whole thing disgusted.

So for a few days, the bike is running well, and only for a few days! Soon, I find 3 broken spokes, and then soon after that, 4 more broken spokes. These rear wheels are definitely a big problem.

I am NOT about to order another wheel. I look into finding different wheels and I found some after being recommended by Rosa to call Bikeberry.com. These are custom, large spoke wheels with only six heavy-duty spokes and they look terrific. The price: $125.00 for the set.

These wheels came with new rotors (smaller) and new calipers. After installing the wheel, it turns out the rear rotor is too small to even reach the caliper and I now have a great-looking bike that runs like a top, with no back brakes! Not only that, but although the front wheel lined up perfectly, it had no stopping power.

Finally, everything is upgraded. I replaced most of the screws from the Chinese garbage to new, made in the USA screws with theadlock added; upgraded the clutch to a Hilliard; the wheels; the engines new; let's go for a ride...

...I get off the bike and immediately notice my chain tensioner is gone. GREAT! I can't ride the bike again! I ordered a new one. A couple of days later I checked the tracking on the new tensioner and the PO Internet tells me they delivered it somewhere in Texas the previous day!

So, I call Gasbike again and wait the typical 2 hours for a callback, that's if one even comes at all. I got Lorenzo on the phone and no; I said nothing about him never calling me back. But he confirmed that the new tensioner went to the wrong address.

Bummer.< /text>< pictures>

<user_name>Brandon Leuner< /user_name><Date>1618980696893<//Date>< Text>
My wife and I contacted Ship2TW for moving from San Francisco to Taipei earlier this year and have had a fantastic experience due to the very helpful staff. Specifically, Lydia, Nicole, and Sally have all been great from start to finish.

After self-packing our things and making an inventory list, we received a quote for pick-up, transport, storage, and final delivery (significantly less than several other shipping companies). Pick-up service was quick and easy, and the staff were very communicative about the status of our shipment in each step of the freight's journey. They were also very accommodating with our request to move the delivery date after the shipment was in transit, and dealt directly with Taiwan Customs for us.

Would definitely recommend Ship2TW and will use them again.<//Text>

<user>117259915990657865314<//user><Name>Lillian Yu Ting Hung</Name><Date>1618392088934< /Date><rate>3</rate>< Text>
I contacted Ship2TW to ship my 40 boxes from the US to Taiwan based on the glowing Google reviews. They were able to make it happen at the end of the day. However, the process was not as smooth as I expected. First of all, when I had all the boxes packed and the packing list prepared, I emailed them multiple times without a response. I had to call them for them to give me a quote, which is fine, at least they got back to me. The contract was signed on December 8. The truck company they contracted with told me on the 17th that they were not able to find a trucker to pick up our boxes. We had only three business days left to get these sorted out as we were leaving town on the 23rd. My husband and I had to drop off all the work we were doing and started calling one freight company after another. As you can imagine, most freight companies don‚Äôt ship household items or require things loaded in pallets. The companies that Ship2TW were trying to reach out to were no help either. I ended up having to contact UPS and enter the dimensions and weight of every single one of our boxes, print all the labels (I had to go to the local print shop as our printer was packed already) and glue them one by one. I understand there was COVID and holiday season going on, but that was a known circumstance already when the contract was signed. I am surprised that there was no backup plan from Ship2TW and we had to go through all the hassle and pay extra money for shipping on top of the amount we had to pay Ship2TW already. Maybe my experience is rare but I still want to share it just so people can have a balanced view of their service. That being said, I still want to thank the staff who have helped us in the process - Lydia, Dores, and Nicole. I appreciate their time and effort sincerely.< /Text>

In order to move from Arizona to Taiwan, I found this company on the Internet. Their website provides a lot of free shipping-related information. After reading it, they decided to call them and then decided to use the company's services. The entire service process can be said to be the best. If you plan to ship your luggage to Taiwan, I highly recommend the services of this company.

(Original)
Moving from AZ to Taiwan. Found this company online. Its website provides lots of free information even before one becomes their customer. I gave them a call decided to use their service, and the whole experience is great as anyone could imagine. They have teams both in the US and Taiwan coordinating the whole process. < Review>
Ko Hyang Korean BBQ is a fairly large restaurant. They offer a typical menu of traditional Korean dishes: Galbi, Bulgogi, spicy pork, spicy chicken, bibimbap, etc. The food itself is good. The banchan..the side dishes are also pretty good. However, service is not the best: most times, staff are less than friendly and not the easiest to get hold of. While the restaurant is typically busy and could use extra help, it isn't an excuse for lack of good customer service.< /Review>

< review>
Came to Ko Hyang this past weekend because the Young Dong's was SUPER packed and Ko Hyang got us in right away! YAY FOR NO WAIT :) The service was pretty quick and attentive.  I really did enjoy the complimentary ban chan, especially the fish cake!! I ordered the bibambap, which came with a bowl of rice on the side and soup.  This was just alright for me, but very filling.  I even had quite a bit left over...which is pretty rare for me.  Overall, not the best place, but if you're just looking to get your tofu soup/korean fix without a long wait and at decent prices, this place is worth stopping by.</review>
